Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: piano\\ \tt RIGHT: hedgehog\\ \tt TOP: tulip\\ \tt BOTTOM: flute\\ \tt CENTER: harps\\ \tt NORTHWEST: saucepan\\ \tt NORTHEAST: lipstick\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: apples\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: copper\\ \tt HERE: primer\\ \tt THERE: pencil sharpener\\ \tt NOWHERE: ukulele\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: pencil case\\ \tt INSIDE: chalk\\ \tt OUTSIDE: daffodil\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }

	 Answer is correct. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 End probing 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 Game finished. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

\end{supertabular}
}
